        <meta property="og:url" content="https://pubs.acs.org/doi/full/10.1021/acsami.9b03279"><meta property="og:title" content="Effect of Conducting Salts in Ionic Liquid Electrolytes for Enhanced Cyclability of Sodium-Ion Batteries"><meta property="og:image" content="https://pubs.acs.org/cms/10.1021/acsami.9b03279/asset/images/acsami.9b03279.social.jpeg_v03"><meta property="og:description" content="The electrochemical performance of ionic liquid electrolytes containing different sodium salts dissolved in 1-butyl-1-methylpyrrolidinium bis(trifluoromethylsulfonyl)imide (BMPTFSI) evaluated in a half-cell configuration using spherical P2-Na0.6Co0.1Mn0.9O2+z (NCO) cathodes are reported. Among the various electrolytes investigated, sodium bis(fluorosulfonyl)imide (NaFSI) (0.5 M) in BMPTFSI shows the best electrochemical performance with a significant improvement in cycling stability (90% capacity retention after 500 cycles at 50 mA g–1 in a half cell versus Na metal anode) compared with conventional NaClO4 (1 M) in ethylene carbonate/propylene carbonate electrolytes (39% retention after 500 cycles). Cyclic voltammetry (CV) studies reveal that ionic liquid electrolytes are stable up to 4.8 V versus Na/Na+. When NaFSI and NaTFSI are used as conducting salts, X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy results prove that the cathode electrolyte interface (CEI) is composed of components resulting from the decomposition of the TFSI anion and the deposition of the BMP cation. On the other hand, the CEI layer of the electrode cycled in an electrolyte containing NaClO4 in BMPTFSI follows a different pathway of TFSI decomposition and consists mainly of sodium fluoride. Similarly, plating studies were used to understand the stability of different ionic liquids in contact with metallic sodium. It was found that the excellent capacity retention for the electrolyte consisting of NaFSI salt is related to the formation of a stable CEI and solid electrolyte interphase layers."><meta property="og:type" content="Article"><meta property="og:site_name" content="ACS Publications"><meta name="twitter:card" content="summary_large_image"><meta name="twitter:site" content="@ACSPublications"><meta name="twitter:image" content="https://pubs.acs.org/cms/10.1021/acsami.9b03279/asset/images/acsami.9b03279.social.jpeg_v03">

<!-- loading Javascript for using the persistence Service -->
    <script src="/wro/nwyw~thiss-ds.js" async="" nonce="90da90e1ae43b325-SJC"></script>

    <script type="text/javascript" nonce="90da90e1ae43b325-SJC">

        var SeamlessAccessService = {
            spUrl: "/action/ssostart",
            returnURL: window.location.href,
            my_context: 'seamlessaccess.org',
            timeout: 5000,

            getWAYFLessUrl: function (entityId) {
                return this.spUrl + "?idp=" + encodeURIComponent(entityId)
                    + "&redirectUri=" + encodeURIComponent(this.returnURL);
            },
            retrieveEntity: function (ms) {
                var self = this;
                var persistService = new thiss.PersistenceService('https://service.seamlessaccess.org/ps/');

                if (ms == undefined || ms === '') {
                    ms = this.timeout;
                }

                return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
                    persistService.entities(self.my_context)
                        .then(function (res) {
                            return resolve(res.data);
                        }, function (err) {
                            // failed
                            reject('failed to retrieve entity from local storage: ' + err);
                        });
                    // Set up the timeout
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        reject('Promise timed out ' + ms + ' ms');
                    }, ms);
                });
            },
            updateEntity: function (entitydata) {
                var self = this;
                var persistService = new thiss.PersistenceService('https://service.seamlessaccess.org/ps/');

                var jsonObj = {};
                try {
                    //try to parse it, if it is a json string
                    jsonObj = JSON.parse(entitydata.val());
                } catch (e) {
                    jsonObj = entitydata;
                }
                return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
                    persistService.update(self.my_context, jsonObj)
                        .then(function (res) {
                            // Process the results
                            var ssoInstitutions = res.data;
                            return resolve(ssoInstitutions);
                        }, function (err) {
                            // failed
                            console.log('failed to update the local storage due to: ' + err);
                            reject(err);
                        });
                })
            },
            removeEntity: function (entityId) {
                var self = this;
                var persistService = new thiss.PersistenceService('https://service.seamlessaccess.org/ps/');

                return new Promise(function (resolve) {
                    persistService.remove(self.my_context, entityId)
                        .then(function (res) {
                            return resolve(res);
                        }, function (err) {
                            // failed
                            console.log('failed to remove from local storage duo to: ' + err);
                        });
                })
            },
            getAccessibleEntityStatus: function (doi, entityId, entityTitle) {
                return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
                    $.ajax({
                        type: 'POST',
                        url: '/action/seamlessAccess',
                        accept: {
                            text: "application/json"
                        },
                        data: {
                            doi: doi,
                            entityid: entityId,
                            entityTitle: entityTitle,
                            eventGroupKey: 'd7f0c4f8-b360-470c-aedb-9e37dcc19a01'
                        }

                    }).done(function (status) {
                        return resolve(status);
                    }).fail(function (status) {
                        return reject(status);
                    });
                });
            },
            getEntitiesWithAllInfo: function (doi) {
                let self = this,
                    arrayOfPromises = [];
                return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
                    self.retrieveEntity().then(function (res) {
                        let allSsoInstitutions = res;
                        for (i = 0; i < allSsoInstitutions.length; i++) {
                            let ssoInstitution = allSsoInstitutions[i];
                            arrayOfPromises.push(new Promise(function (resolve) {
                                self.getAccessibleEntityStatus(doi, ssoInstitution.entity.entityID, ssoInstitution.entity.title)
                                    .then(function (entityStatus) {
                                        resolve({
                                            entityID: ssoInstitution.entity.entityID,
                                            entityTitle: ssoInstitution.entity.title,
                                            entityStatusObj: entityStatus,
                                            entitySsoUrl: self.getWAYFLessUrl(ssoInstitution.entity.entityID)
                                        });
                                    }, function (err) {
                                        console.log('failed to get the entity status: ' + ssoInstitution.entity.entityID,err);
                                    });
                            }));
                        }
                        if(allSsoInstitutions.length === 0 && true){
                            self.getAccessibleEntityStatus(doi, null, null)
                                .then(function () {
                                    console.log('No Entity found');
                                }, function (err) {
                                    console.log('failed to get the none entity status' ,err);
                                });
                        }
                        Promise.all(arrayOfPromises)
                            .then(function (finalResponse) {
                                resolve(finalResponse);
                            }).catch(function (err) {
                                reject(err);
                            });

                    }).catch(function (err) {
                        reject(err);
                    })
                });
            }
        };

        window.addEventListener('load', function () {
            document.querySelectorAll(".sso-institution").forEach(function (institution) {
                var entityId = institution.getAttribute('data-entityid');
                var entityName = institution.getAttribute('data-name');
                var entitydata = {
                    entityID: entityId,
                    title: entityName
                };
                institution.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
                    e.preventDefault();

                    if ($('.institution-preference-userconsent-checkbox').length > 0) {
                        let institutionPreferenceUserConsentCheckbox = $('.institution-preference-userconsent-checkbox').get(0);
                        if (!$(institutionPreferenceUserConsentCheckbox).is(":checked")) {
                            return;
                        }
                    }

                    var self = this;
                    SeamlessAccessService.updateEntity(entitydata).then(function (res) {
                        console.log(res);
                        window.location.href = self.href;
                    }).catch(function (err) {
                        window.location.href = self.href;
                    });
                });
            });
        });

    </script>

type="text/x-mathjax-config;executed=true">MathJax.Hub.Config({
            menuSettings: {
                zoom: "Click",
                zscale: "150%"
            },
            SVG: {
                fonts: ["STIX-Web"],
                linebreaks: { automatic: true },
            },
            "HTML-CSS": {
                fonts: ["STIX"],
                linebreaks: { automatic: true },
                scale: 90,
            },
        });

        MathJax.Hub.Register.StartupHook("mml Jax Ready", function () {
            var MML = MathJax.ElementJax.mml;
            MML.mi.prototype.setTeXclass = function (prev) {
                this.getPrevClass(prev);
                return this;
            };
            MML.mfrac.Augment({
                setTeXclass: function (prev) {
                    this.getPrevClass(prev);
                    for (var i = 0, m = this.data.length; i < m; i++) {
                        if (this.data[i]) this.data[i].setTeXclass();
                    }
                    return this;
                }
            });
        });

        MathJax.Hub.Register.StartupHook("SVG Jax Ready", function () {
            var FONT = MathJax.OutputJax.SVG.FONTDATA.VARIANT["-STIX-Web-variant"] || MathJax.OutputJax.SVG.FONTDATA.VARIANT["-STIX-variant"];
            delete MathJax.ElementJax.mml.mo.prototype.remapChars['°'];
            if (FONT) {
                FONT.remap[0xB0]= [0x25E6, "normal"];
                FONT.remap[0x2A]= [0x2217, "normal"];
            }

        });

        MathJax.Hub.Register.StartupHook("MathML Jax Ready", function () {
            var PARSE = MathJax.InputJax.MathML.Parse;
            var ADD = PARSE.prototype.AddChildren;
            PARSE.Augment({
                AddChildren: function (mml, node) {
                    ADD.call(this, mml, node);
                    if (mml.type === 'mrow') {
                        var first = mml.data[0], last = mml.data[mml.data.length-1];
                        if (mml.open && !mml.data[0].Get('stretchy')) delete mml.open;
                        if (mml.close && !mml.data[mml.data.length - 1].Get('stretchy')) delete mml.close;
                    }
                }
            });
        });

        MathJax.Hub.Register.StartupHook("HTML-CSS Jax Ready", function () {
            var HTMLCSS = MathJax.OutputJax['HTML-CSS'];
            var DELIMITERS = HTMLCSS.FONTDATA.DELIMITERS;
            var FONT = HTMLCSS.FONTDATA.VARIANT["-STIX-variant"] || HTMLCSS.FONTDATA.VARIANT["-STIX-Web-variant"]

            var MML = MathJax.ElementJax.mml;

            MML.mrow.Augment({
              _HTMLlineBreaks: MML.mrow.prototype.HTMLlineBreaks,
              HTMLlineBreaks: function (span) {

                if (this.parent.linebreakContainer && this.Get("display") === "inline") return false;
                return this._HTMLlineBreaks(span);
              }
            });


            DELIMITERS[0x0305] = {dir: "H", alias: 0x00AF};
            DELIMITERS[0x033F] = {dir: "H", alias: 0x003D};
            DELIMITERS[0x20E1] = {dir: "H", alias: 0x2194};

            if (FONT) {
                FONT.remap[0xB0]= [0x25E6, "normal"];
                FONT.remap[0x2A]= [0x2217, "normal"];
            }

            delete MathJax.ElementJax.mml.mo.prototype.remapChars['°'];
        });

        MathJax.Hub.Register.StartupHook("HTML-CSS multiline Ready", function () {
            var HTMLCSS = MathJax.OutputJax["HTML-CSS"];
            var MML = MathJax.ElementJax.mml;
            var PENALTY = MML.mbase.prototype.HTMLlinebreakPenalty;

            MML.msqrt.Augment({
                linebreakContainer: false,
                HTMLbetterBreak: function () {return false}
            });
            MML.mroot.Augment({
                linebreakContainer: false,
                HTMLbetterBreak: function () {return false}
            });
            MML.mfrac.Augment({
                linebreakContainer: false,
                HTMLbetterBreak: function () {return false}
            });
            MML.mspace.Augment({
                defaultDef: {
                    indentalign: MML.INDENTALIGN.AUTO,
                    indentshift: "0",
                    indenttarget: "",
                    indentalignfirst: MML.INDENTALIGN.INDENTALIGN,
                    indentshiftfirst: MML.INDENTSHIFT.INDENTSHIFT,
                    indentalignlast: MML.INDENTALIGN.INDENTALIGN,
                    indentshiftlast: MML.INDENTSHIFT.INDENTSHIFT
                },
                HTMLbetterBreak: function (info,state) {
                    if (info.values && info.values.id === this.spanID) {return false}
                    var values = this.getValues(
                        "linebreak",
                        "indentalign","indentshift",
                        "indentalignfirst","indentshiftfirst",
                        "indentalignlast","indentshiftlast"
                    );
                    var linebreakValue = values.linebreak;
                    if (!linebreakValue || this.hasDimAttr()) {
                        linebreakValue = MML.LINEBREAK.AUTO;
                    }
                    var W = info.scanW, span = this.HTMLspanElement(), w = span.bbox.w;
                    if (span.style.paddingLeft) {w += HTMLCSS.unEm(span.style.paddingLeft)}
                    if (W - info.shift === 0) {return false} // don't break at zero width
                    var offset = HTMLCSS.linebreakWidth - W;

                    if (state.n === 0 && (values.indentshiftfirst !== state.VALUES.indentshiftfirst ||
                        values.indentalignfirst !== state.VALUES.indentalignfirst)) {
                        var align = this.HTMLgetAlign(state,values),
                            shift = this.HTMLgetShift(state,values,align);
                        offset += (info.shift - shift);
                    }

                    var penalty = Math.floor(offset / HTMLCSS.linebreakWidth * 1000);
                    if (penalty < 0) {penalty = PENALTY.toobig - 3*penalty}
                    penalty += info.nest * PENALTY.nestfactor;

                    var linebreak = PENALTY[linebreakValue]||0;
                    if (linebreakValue === MML.LINEBREAK.AUTO && w >= PENALTY.spacelimit &&
                        !this.mathbackground && !this.background)
                    {linebreak = [(w+PENALTY.spaceoffset)*PENALTY.spacefactor]}
                    if (!MathJax.Object.isArray(linebreak)) {
                        if (linebreak || offset >= 0) {penalty = linebreak * info.nest}
                    } else {penalty = Math.max(1,penalty + linebreak[0] * info.nest)}

                    if (penalty >= info.penalty) {return false}
                    info.penalty = penalty; info.values = values; info.W = W; info.w = w;
                    values.lineleading = state.VALUES.lineleading;
                    values.linebreakstyle = "before"; values.id = this.spanID;
                    return true;
                }
            });


            
            PENALTY.goodbreak = [-400];

<script type="text/javascript" nonce="90da90e1ae43b325-SJC">
var dfpReady = false;
$(document).ready(function() {
    // var journalTitle = 'applied_materials_interfaces';
    var taxonomyKeywords = $('.article_header-taxonomy');
    var articleKeyword = $('meta[name="keywords"]');
    var articleTitle = $('meta[name="dc.Title"]');
    var articleDescription = $('meta[name="dc.Description"]');
    var abstractKeyword = $('p.articleBody_abstractText:contains("Keywords: ")');
    var searchTerms = [];

    if (taxonomyKeywords.length > 0) {
        $(taxonomyKeywords).children(".rlist--inline").children("li").each(function() {
            searchTerms.push($(this).text());
        });
    }
    else if (articleKeyword.length > 0) { 
        searchTerms = searchTerms.concat(articleKeyword.prop('content').split(', '));
    }
    else if (abstractKeyword.length > 0) {
        searchTerms = searchTerms.concat(abstractKeyword.text().split("Keywords: ")[1].split('; '));
    }
    else if (articleDescription.length > 0) {
        $(articleDescription).each(function() {
            articleDescriptionKeywords = $(this).prop('content');
            articleDescriptionKeywords = articleDescriptionKeywords.replace(/.,/g,"");
            articleDescriptionKeywords = articleDescriptionKeywords.replace(/\s{2,}/g," ");
            searchTerms = searchTerms.concat(articleDescriptionKeywords.split(' '));
        });
    }

    if (articleTitle.length > 0) {
        searchTerms = searchTerms.concat(articleTitle.prop('content').split(' '));
    }

    googletag.cmd.push(function() {
        var mappingLeader = googletag.sizeMapping().
        addSize([750, 200], [728, 90]). 
        addSize([0, 0], [320, 50]).
        build();
        //leaderboard
        googletag.defineSlot('/8868/journal/applied_materials_interfaces/article', [728, 90], 'dfp-journal-article-leaderboard').defineSizeMapping(mappingLeader).setTargeting('location', 'leaderboard1').setTargeting('Keyword', searchTerms).addService(googletag.pubads());
        //recommend
        googletag.defineSlot("/8868/journal/applied_materials_interfaces/article", [1, 1], "dfp-journal-article-recommend").setTargeting("ntvPlacement", ["1100167"]).setTargeting("location", "recommend").setTargeting('Keyword', searchTerms).addService(googletag.pubads());
        //googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
        googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs();
        googletag.pubads().setTargeting('inst',dartInstitutionType).setTargeting('memb',dartMember);
        googletag.pubads().addEventListener("slotRenderEnded", function(event) {
            console.log(event.slot.getSlotElementId() + " isEmpty: " + event.isEmpty + " | creative id: " + event.creativeId + " " + event.size[0] + "x" + event.size[1]);
            if((event.isEmpty === false) && (event.slot.getSlotElementId() != "dfp-journal-article-recommend")) {
                $("#" + event.slot.getSlotElementId()).parents(".advertisement").slideDown();
                console.log("ad display: " + event.creativeId + " " + event.size[0] + "x" + event.size[1]);
            }
            // else {
            //     console.log("no ad found");
            // }
        });
        googletag.enableServices();
        dfpReady = true;
    });
});
</script>

<script nonce="90da90e1ae43b325-SJC">
$(function() {
    var serialCode = "aamick";
    var books = ["reagents", "symposium", "advances", "medichemreviews", "styleguide"]
    if(books.includes(serialCode) === false) {
        // default click action
        $("[data-id]").on("mousedown", function(e) {
            var currentClickID = $(this).attr("data-id");

            if(currentClickID.includes("_hover") === false) {
                if(currentClickID.match("^article_") && !currentClickID.match("^article_abstract_CC")) {   
                    gtag('event', "Journal Article", { "Article_Title": "Effect of Conducting Salts in Ionic Liquid Electrolytes for Enhanced Cyclability of Sodium-Ion Batteries", "Article_DOI": "10.1021/acsami.9b03279", "Article_Element": $(this).attr("data-id") });
                }
            }
        });
        
        // Access Management icons hover
        var articleAccessManagementIconHover = false;
        var articleAccessManagementIconHoverEvent = false;
        $("[data-id='article_access_icon']").on("mouseenter", function(e) {
            if(articleAccessManagementIconHoverEvent === false) {
                articleAccessManagementIconHover = true;
                var articleAccessManagementHover =  $(this).attr("data-id") + "_hover";
                
                setTimeout(function() { 
                    if(articleAccessManagementIconHover === true) {
                        gtag("event", "Journal Article", { "Article_Title": "Effect of Conducting Salts in Ionic Liquid Electrolytes for Enhanced Cyclability of Sodium-Ion Batteries", "Article_DOI": "10.1021/acsami.9b03279", "Article_Element": articleAccessManagementHover });
    
                        articleAccessManagementIconHoverEvent = true;
                    }
                }, 1000);
            }
        });
        $("[data-id='article_access_icon']").on("mouseleave", function(e) {
            articleAccessManagementIconHover = false;
        });
    
        // articleRightsPermissionsLink hover
        var articleRightsPermissionsLinkHover = false;
        var articleRightsPermissionsLinkHoverEvent = false;
        $("[data-id='article_rights_permissions']").on("mouseenter", function(e) {
            if(articleRightsPermissionsLinkHoverEvent === false) {
                articleRightsPermissionsLinkHover = true;
                var articleRightsHover =  $(this).attr("data-id") + "_hover";
                
                setTimeout(function() { 
                    if(articleRightsPermissionsLinkHover === true) {
                        gtag("event", "Journal Article", { "Article_Title": "Effect of Conducting Salts in Ionic Liquid Electrolytes for Enhanced Cyclability of Sodium-Ion Batteries", "Article_DOI": "10.1021/acsami.9b03279", "Article_Element": articleRightsHover });
    
                        articleRightsPermissionsLinkHoverEvent = true;
                    }
                }, 1000);
            }
        });
        $("[data-id='article_rights_permissions']").on("mouseleave", function(e) {
            articleRightsPermissionsLinkHover = false;
        });
    
        // Author hover
        var articleAuthorHover = false
        var articleAuthorHoverEvent = false
        $("[data-id='article_author_info']").on("mouseenter", function(e) {
            if((articleAuthorHoverEvent === false) && ($(this).parent().hasClass("view-affs") === false)) {
                articleAuthorHover = true;
                var authorInfoHover =  $(this).attr("data-id") + "_hover";
                
                setTimeout(function() { 
                    if((articleAuthorHover === true) && (articleAuthorHoverEvent === false)) {
                        gtag("event", "Journal Article", { "Article_Title": "Effect of Conducting Salts in Ionic Liquid Electrolytes for Enhanced Cyclability of Sodium-Ion Batteries", "Article_DOI": "10.1021/acsami.9b03279", "Article_Element": authorInfoHover });
    
                        articleAuthorHoverEvent = true;
                    }
                }, 1000);
            }
        });
        $("[data-id='article_author_info']").on("mouseleave", function(e) {
            articleAuthorHover = false;
        });
    
        // CC License hover
        var articleAbstractCCHover = false
        var articleAbstractCCHoverEvent = false
        var articleDrawerCCHover = false
        var articleDrawerCCHoverEvent = false
        $(".article__cc-license__inter a").on("mouseenter", function(e) {
            if($(this).attr("data-id")) {
                if(($(this).attr("data-id") === "article_drawer_CC-License") && (articleDrawerCCHoverEvent === false)) {
                    articleDrawerCCHover = true;
                    
                    setTimeout(function() { 
                        if((articleDrawerCCHover === true) && (articleDrawerCCHoverEvent === false)) {
                            gtag("event", "Journal Article", { "Article_Title": "Effect of Conducting Salts in Ionic Liquid Electrolytes for Enhanced Cyclability of Sodium-Ion Batteries", "Article_DOI": "10.1021/acsami.9b03279", "Article_Element": "article_drawer_CC-License_hover" });
    
                            articleDrawerCCHoverEvent = true;
                        }
                    }, 1000);
                }
                else if(($(this).attr("data-id").match("^article_abstract_CC")) && (articleAbstractCCHoverEvent === false)) {
                    articleAbstractCCHover = true;
    
                    setTimeout(function() { 
                        if((articleAbstractCCHover === true) && (articleAbstractCCHoverEvent === false)) {
                            gtag("event", "Journal Article", { "Article_Title": "Effect of Conducting Salts in Ionic Liquid Electrolytes for Enhanced Cyclability of Sodium-Ion Batteries", "Article_DOI": "10.1021/acsami.9b03279", "Article_Element": "article_abstract_CC_hover" });
    
                            articleAbstractCCHoverEvent = true;
                        }
                    }, 1000);
                }
            }
            else if(($(this).hasClass("article__cc-license__link")) && (articleAbstractCCHoverEvent === false)) {
                articleAbstractCCHover = true;
                
                setTimeout(function() { 
                    if((articleAbstractCCHover === true) && (articleAbstractCCHoverEvent === false)) {
                        gtag("event", "Journal Article", { "Article_Title": "Effect of Conducting Salts in Ionic Liquid Electrolytes for Enhanced Cyclability of Sodium-Ion Batteries", "Article_DOI": "10.1021/acsami.9b03279", "Article_Element": "article_abstract_CC_hover" });
    
                        articleAbstractCCHoverEvent = true;
                    }
                }, 1000);
            }
        });
        $(".article__cc-license__inter a").on("mouseleave", function(e) {
            if(articleAbstractCCHover === true) {
                articleAbstractCCHover = false;
            }
            if(articleDrawerCCHover = true) {
                articleDrawerCCHover = false;
            }
        });
        
        // show recommeneded click delay
        var intervalCount = 0;
        var showRecommendedInterval = setInterval(function() {
            intervalCount += 100;
            if($(".show-recommended__wrapper .show-recommended").length > 0) {
                clearInterval(showRecommendedInterval);
                $("[data-id='article_drawer_RecommendedShowMore']").on("mousedown", function(e) {
                    gtag('event', "Journal Article", { "Article_Title": "Effect of Conducting Salts in Ionic Liquid Electrolytes for Enhanced Cyclability of Sodium-Ion Batteries", "Article_DOI": "10.1021/acsami.9b03279", "Article_Element": $(this).attr("data-id") });
                });
                $("[data-id='article_drawer_RecommendedShowLess']").on("mousedown", function(e) {
                    gtag('event', "Journal Article", { "Article_Title": "Effect of Conducting Salts in Ionic Liquid Electrolytes for Enhanced Cyclability of Sodium-Ion Batteries", "Article_DOI": "10.1021/acsami.9b03279", "Article_Element": $(this).attr("data-id") });
                });
            }
        }, 100);
    }
});
</script>

Kühn</a></span></div><div class="loa-info-orcid"><img height="20" width="27" src="/products/achs/releasedAssets/images/orchid-2856f829046fbda55b90e1582edf0e9a.png" alt="Orcid"><a href="http://orcid.org/0000-0002-4156-780X" title="Orcid link">http://orcid.org/0000-0002-4156-780X</a></div></div></div></span></li><li><span><span class="hlFld-ContribAuthor" tabindex="0" data-id="article_author_info" property="author">Madhavi Srinivasan</span><strong>*</strong><div class="loa-info hlFld-Affiliation"><div class="loa-info--wrapper"><div class="loa-info-name">Madhavi Srinivasan</div><div class="loa-info-affiliations"><div class="loa-info-affiliations-info">School of Materials Science and Engineering, Nanyang Technological University, Singapore 639798, Singapore</div></div><span class="conrtib-corresp"><strong>*</strong>E-mail: <a href="mailto:madhavi@ntu.edu.sg">madhavi@ntu.edu.sg</a>. Phone: (65) 6790-4606. Fax: (65) 6790-9081.</span><span class="conrtib-corresp"></span><div class="loa-info-scifinder"><span>More by <a href="/action/doSearch?field1=Contrib&amp;text1=Madhavi++Srinivasan" data-id="article_author_search">Madhavi Srinivasan</a></span></div></div></div></span></li></ul><div class="article_header-footer"><div class="article_header-footer-left"><div class="article_header-links"><input class="pub-doi" type="hidden" name="pub-doi" value="10.1021/acsami.9b03279"><a href="/doi/epdf/10.1021/acsami.9b03279?ref=article_openPDF" title="PDF" target="_blank" class="article__btn__secondary" data-id="article_header_OpenPDF"><i class="icon-open-pdf"></i><span>Open PDF</span></a><a href="#_i21" title="Supporting Information" class="article__btn__secondary internalNav" data-id="article_header_SupportingInfo"><i class="icon-supporting-info"></i><span>Supporting Information (1)</span></a><a href="/servlet/linkout?suffix=s0&amp;dbid=16384&amp;doi=10.1021/acsami.9b03279&amp;type=refOpenUrl&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fimp-primo.hosted.exlibrisgroup.com%2Fopenurl%2F44IMP%2FICL_VU1%3Fid%3Ddoi%3A10.1021%252Facsami.9b03279%26sid%3Dliteratum%253Aachs%26pmid%3D31251014%26genre%3Darticle%26aulast%3DDo%26date%3D2019%26atitle%3DEffect%2Bof%2BConducting%2BSalts%2Bin%2BIonic%2BLiquid%2BElectrolytes%2Bfor%2BEnhanced%2BCyclability%2Bof%2BSodium-Ion%2BBatteries%26jtitle%3DACS%2BApplied%2BMaterials%2B%2526%2BInterfaces%26title%3DACS%2BApplied%2BMaterials%2B%2526%2BInterfaces%26volume%3D11%26issue%3D27%26spage%3D23972%26epage%3D23981%26issn%3D1944-8244" title="OpenURL IMPERIAL COLLEGE LONDON" class="issue-item_open-url sfxLink"><img src="/userimages/9157ccea-6c85-4e5f-ac2a-6a9fd9422c17/sfxbutton-180e067c810" alt="OpenURL IMPERIAL COLLEGE LONDON"></a></div></div></div><div class="article_header-meta"><div class="article_header-meta-left"><input type="hidden" name="journalCodeForjhpLink" value="aamick"><input type="hidden" name="journalNameForjhpLink" value="ACS Applied Materials &amp; class="articleHeaderDropzone4" data-pb-dropzone="articleHeaderDropzone4"><div class="articleRightsPermissionsLink"><a href="/servlet/linkout?type=rightslink&amp;url=startPage%3D23972%26pageCount%3D10%26copyright%3DAmerican%2BChemical%2BSociety%26author%3DMinh%2BPhuong%2BDo%252C%2BNicolas%2BBucher%252C%2BArun%2BNagasubramanian%252C%2Bet%2Bal%26orderBeanReset%3Dtrue%26imprint%3DAmerican%2BChemical%2BSociety%26volumeNum%3D11%26issueNum%3D27%26contentID%3Dacsami.9b03279%26title%3DEffect%2Bof%2BConducting%2BSalts%2Bin%2BIonic%2BLiquid%2BElectrolytes%2Bfor%2BEnhanced%2BCyclability%2Bof%2BSodium-Ion%2BBatteries%26numPages%3D10%26pa%3D%26issn%3D1944-8244%26publisherName%3Dacs%26publication%3Daamick%26rpt%3Dn%26endPage%3D23981%26publicationDate%3DJuly%2B2019" Empty dropzone --></div></div></div></div><div class="article_abstract"><div class="article_abstract-title" id="Abstract" tabindex="0"><h2>Abstract</h2><div class="article__copy"><button class="article__copy__btn"><i class="article__copy__icon icon-copy-solid" aria-hidden="true"></i></button><span class="article__copy__text">Click to copy section link</span><span class="article__copy__success">Section link copied!</span></div></div><div class="article_abstract-content hlFld-Abstract" id="abstractBox" property="description"><figure id="_i1" data-index="0" class="article__inlineFigure article_abstract-img"><button class="figure-viewer__trigger" aria-label="open figure viewer"><img class="inline-fig internalNav" src="/cms/10.1021/acsami.9b03279/asset/images/medium/am-2019-03279m_0009.gif" alt="" id="tgr1" property="image" style="width:405px; height:275px"></button><div class="figure-bottom-links"><div class="download-hi-res-img"><a title="High Resolution Image" href="/cms/10.1021/acsami.9b03279/asset/images/large/am-2019-03279m_0009.jpeg"><span>High Resolution Image</span></a></div><div class="download-ppt"><a title="Download MS PowerPoint Slide" href="/action/downloadFigures?doi=10.1021/acsami.9b03279&amp;id=_i1"><span>Download MS PowerPoint Slide</span></a></div></div></figure><p class="articleBody_abstractText">The electrochemical performance of ionic liquid electrolytes containing different sodium salts dissolved in 1-butyl-1-methylpyrrolidinium bis(trifluoromethylsulfonyl)imide (BMPTFSI) evaluated in a half-cell configuration using spherical P2-Na<sub>0.6</sub>Co<sub>0.1</sub>Mn<sub>0.9</sub>O<sub>2+<i>z</i></sub> (NCO) cathodes are reported. Among the various electrolytes investigated, sodium bis(fluorosulfonyl)imide (NaFSI) (0.5 M) in BMPTFSI shows the best electrochemical performance with a significant improvement in cycling stability (90% capacity retention after 500 cycles at 50 mA g<sup>–1</sup> in a half cell versus Na metal anode) compared with conventional NaClO<sub>4</sub> (1 M) in ethylene carbonate/propylene carbonate electrolytes (39% retention after 500 cycles). Cyclic voltammetry (CV) studies reveal that ionic liquid electrolytes are stable up to 4.8 V versus Na/Na<sup>+</sup>. When NaFSI and NaTFSI are used as conducting salts, X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy results prove that the cathode electrolyte interface (CEI) is composed of components resulting from the decomposition of the TFSI anion and the deposition of the BMP cation. On the other hand, the CEI layer of the electrode cycled in an electrolyte containing NaClO<sub>4</sub> in BMPTFSI follows a different pathway of TFSI decomposition and consists mainly of sodium fluoride. Similarly, plating studies were used to understand the stability of different ionic liquids in contact with metallic sodium. It was found that the excellent capacity retention for the electrolyte consisting of NaFSI salt is related to the formation of a stable CEI and solid electrolyte interphase layers.</p></div><div class="article__cc-license"><div class="article__cc-license__body"><p class="article__cc-license__para">This publication is licensed under the terms of your
                            institutional subscription.
                            <a href="/servlet/linkout?type=rightslink&amp;url=startPage%3D23972%26pageCount%3D10%26copyright%3DAmerican%2BChemical%2BSociety%26author%3DMinh%2BPhuong%2BDo%252C%2BNicolas%2BBucher%252C%2BArun%2BNagasubramanian%252C%2Bet%2Bal%26orderBeanReset%3Dtrue%26imprint%3DAmerican%2BChemical%2BSociety%26volumeNum%3D11%26issueNum%3D27%26contentID%3Dacsami.9b03279%26title%3DEffect%2Bof%2BConducting%2BSalts%2Bin%2BIonic%2BLiquid%2BElectrolytes%2Bfor%2BEnhanced%2BCyclability%2Bof%2BSodium-Ion%2BBatteries%26numPages%3D10%26pa%3D%26issn%3D1944-8244%26publisherName%3Dacs%26publication%3Daamick%26rpt%3Dn%26endPage%3D23981%26publicationDate%3DJuly%2B2019" class="link--bold">Request reuse permissions.</a></p></div></div><span class="hidden" property="publisher">ACS Publications</span><div class="article_header-article-copyright">Copyright © 2019 American Chemical Society</div><div class="article_header-footer-right"><div class="articleHeaderDropzone7" data-pb-dropzone="articleHeaderDropzone7"><!-- Empty dropzone --></div></div><div class="article__tags article__tags--keywords hlFld-Abstract"><div class="article__tags__container"><header class="article__tags__header"><h3 class="article__tags__heading">Keywords</h3><div class="article__tags__tooltip" tabindex="0"><div class="article__tags__icon" aria-describedby="tooltip-keywords"><i class="icon-info-circle-outline"></i><span class="sr-only">what are keywords</span></div><p class="article__tags__diff" id="tooltip-keywords" role="tooltip">
